I enjoyed the moisturizing strips that made the shave a smooth, quick, and simple process. However, when it came to the bikini area I was unable to successfully use the trimming side of the razor simply because I don&#x27;t let my hair &amp;#34;down there&amp;#34; get long enough for the trimmer to work effectively. I ended up just using the razor side to clear off the remaining hair and it worked okay, but still left some stubble. I&#x27;d say for legs, the razor worked incredibly well. The smoothest shave I have ever had with no knicks or cuts; plus the results lasted a few days longer so instead of shaving everyday I only had to shave every 2-3 days. However, for me when it comes to the bikini area the trimmer just wasn&#x27;t effective. Thus, I&#x27;d likely not spend the money on a razor where I can only benefit from one of its functions.</li>

Since the razor has a strip of conditioning serum attached, I was able to just wet my legs in the shower and shave with no razor burns afterward. Note that once the razor is wet, the serum does leave a gooey layer on you as you shave over the area, but it&#x27;s easy to rinse this away in the shower. After getting out of the shower I did not notice my legs being significantly moisturized by the razor&#x27;s serum, but it didn&#x27;t dry my legs out either. Also, I did not experience any allergic reactions.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;On to the bikini trimmer - I was definitely more impressed with this end of the product! The trimmer is turned on by pressing on a button and can be used in the shower or out even though it is AAA-battery powered since it was built to be waterproof. I&#x27;ve used in both inside and out of the shower and while it does work while wet, I prefer to trim outside of the shower as I find it less messy.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The trimmer has 4 length settings, which can be easily adjusted by manually pushing the plastic comb in for a shorter trim length or pulling the comb out for a longer trim. I used the 2nd longest trim length and went over my entire bikini area, trimmed in an upward direction, and am very happy with the results as I think the trimmer thins out the hair more evenly without looking choppy like it would if I used a scissor. I do appreciate that the trimmer helps accumulate the hair in its comb, leaving no mess on the floor and allowing you to pick it all up together with a tissue or wash it away. (This might depend on how much hair there is and how long it is, but this was my experience.) The remaining hair was very easy to clean by removing the comb and rinsing the clipper.  All-in-all, using the Hydro Silk TrimStyle bikini trimmer yielded a straight-forward, easy, and neat trim for me!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The one criticism that stuck out to me is that the razor end does not come with a cover so when using the trimmer I had to be mindful of how I held the product. This is not to say that the razor would easily cut me while I trimmed, but it was just in the back of my mind and a cover may have helped alleviate this concern. Also a cover would be beneficial for storing the razor when I&#x27;m not using the product.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Still, I&#x27;d say that the trimmer makes this product worth it if the product is priced at retail (which I believe is less than $15?)and rinsing the clipper.  All-in-all, using the Hydro Silk TrimStyle bikini trimmer yielded a straight-forward, easy, and neat trim for me!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The one criticism that stuck out to me is that the razor end does not come with a cover so when using the trimmer I had to be mindful of how I held the product.     <li> Got one of these from BzzAgent for review...&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;UPDATED*&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;BLUF: The trimmer is a wonderful product, esp. for the price. However, I dislike the razor so much I had to write a second review (and drop a star).&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This is my second review of this product (my original is below if you&#x27;re super curious). I still love love LOVE the trimmer. It rocks, no kidding. This little trimmer can handle a wet mustache no problems! (Not my mustache, by the way. I convinced a friend to let me experiment on his.) The trimmer is the bomb and if you want a waterproof trimmer the Hydro Schick TrimStyle will meet your needs.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The razor - I kind of can&#x27;t say enough about this, and not in a good way. It really stinks. I&#x27;ve gotten better shaves from disposable razors out of motel vending machines. The ONLY good thing about it is the built in lubricant. That rocks. So long as your skin is wet you can shave with just the razor; no soap or cream required. The quality of your shave, however, may leave you wanting, well, less. After my shave my legs were proudly sporting stubble and hairs that were totally passed over. Around and behind the knee are all prickly. The area on the shin where the shin bone and the calf muscle meet is impossible to get with this razor. That tiny dip is enough to keep this razor from meeting the skin; even if you turn the razor sideways and try shaving at an angle.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;My friend tried to shave his face with it and he experienced the same results. There is lots of stubble under his chin and even on his cheeks! The cheek stubble was really surprising because he has full, smooth cheeks that should have been perfect for a close shave. This razor just doesn&#x27;t cut it. (joke option!)&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In short; if you want a trimmer, TrimStyle is for you. It&#x27;s small, portable, easy to use. If, on the other hand, you are looking for a razor; keep looking.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Please see my original review for more detail on the specs and function of the TrimStyle.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------&lt;br /&gt;Original review:&lt;br /&gt;Alright you lovely people, here&#x27;s the deal: This little trimmer rocks! I&#x27;ll be honest here, I didn&#x27;t try it on myself as I have nothing to trim. Instead I went one better and grabbed a friend who sports a mustache-goatee combo. He kindly stood still while I buzzed his face. We were both very impressed by how smoothly everything went. No snagging, pulling, clogging. It was quick and painless! The trimmer is about 1 inch wide; just perfect for delicate work. The adjustable head does allow for a bit of control over hair length but not a lot. The longest length is around .5 inches (perfect for a mustache goatee.) My friend actually dropped by my house yesterday to borrow the trimmer. It&#x27;s a winner! Now, about the razor. Honestly, I wasn&#x27;t super impressed. It gives a close, smooth shave. The built-in moisturizer is beyond awesome! If you&#x27;ve ever used fresh aloe (the slimy insides of the actual leaf) then you know what the moisturizer strip feels like. I was actually able to shave using only the lubricant provided by the razor head. It&#x27;s really nice. The caveat is that you can only use it on your legs (and even then it&#x27;s hit-or-miss behind the knees). Forget working on your bikini area with that enormous razor head. And don&#x27;t expect a smooth finish under your arms. The 5 blades are a boon. The plastic monstrosity that encases them is not. The razor head is so large that you simply cannot get into any areas where your skin creases. Now I know this is getting picky, but the packaging on this thing is not very well done. It comes in a standard cardboard box with clear plastic inserts. However, to get the razor out you have to rip the box open. Neither the top nor the bottom opens easily. All of the sides have been glued down. This is not a terrible thing except that the instructions have been printed on theinside of the box and can be (were) easily torn. Please, Schick, add an access point! The other issue that I have is the lack of a cleaning brush. The trimmer head disassembles very nicely and is completely waterproof. Hairs, on the other hand, tend to stick when they get wet meaning that running the trimmer under water does not actually get it clean. I had to use an old tooth brush to remove the excess hair. It&#x27;s a $15 product (plus or minus) but adding a $.20 brush should be do able. Personally, I&#x27;m not keen on needing 2 separate razors to get the job done. I will continue using my current razor which works for legs, bikini, and under arms. The trimmer is excellent and will likely be moving into its new home as a stache-trimmer ;) If you are looking for a good multi-purpose tool the Hydro Silk TrimStyle is close, but not quite there yet.&lt;br /&gt;Now, about the razor. Honestly, I wasn&#x27;t super impressed. It gives a close, smooth shave. The built-in moisturizer is beyond awesome! If you&#x27;ve ever used fresh aloe (the slimy insides of the actual leaf) then you know what the moisturizer strip feels like. I was actually able to shave using only the lubricant provided by the razor head. It&#x27;s really nice. The caveat is that you can only use it on your legs (and even then it&#x27;s hit-or-miss behind the knees). Forget working on your bikini area with that enormous razor head. And don&#x27;t expect a smooth finish under your arms. The 5 blades are a boon. The plastic monstrosity that encases them is not. The razor head is so large that you simply cannot get into any areas where your skin creases.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Now I know this is getting picky, but the packaging on this thing is not very well done. If you&#x27;ve ever used fresh aloe (the slimy insides of the actual leaf) then you know what the moisturizer strip feels like. I was actually able to shave using only the lubricant provided by the razor head. It&#x27;s really nice. The caveat is that you can only use it on your legs (and even then it&#x27;s hit-or-miss behind the knees). Forget working on your bikini area with that enormous razor head. And don&#x27;t expect a smooth finish under your arms. The 5 blades are a boon. The plastic monstrosity that encases them is not. The razor head is so large that you simply cannot get into any areas where your skin creases.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Now I know this is getting picky, but the packaging on this thing is not very well done. It comes in a standard cardboard box with clear plastic inserts. However, to get the razor out you have to rip the box open. Neither the top nor the bottom opens easily. All of the sides have been glued down. This is not a terrible thing except that the instructions have been printed on the inside of the box and can be (were) easily torn. Please, Schick, add an access point!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The other issue that I have is the lack of a cleaning brush. The trimmer head disassembles very nicely and is completely waterproof. Hairs, on the other hand, tend to stick when they get wet meaning that running the trimmer under water does not actually get it clean. I had to use an old tooth brush to remove the excess hair. It&#x27;s a $15 product (plus or minus) but adding a $.20 brush should be do able.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Personally, I&#x27;m not keen on needing 2 separate razors to get the job done. I will continue using my current razor which works for legs, bikini, and under arms. The trimmer is excellent and will likely be moving into its new home as a stache-trimmer ;)  If you are looking for a good multi-purpose tool the Hydro Silk TrimStyle is close, but not quite there yet.</li>

The button was a bit difficult to turn on/off, but not terribly difficult or inconvenient. Even though shaving is NOT one of my favorite beauty regimens, I was excited to give it a try. In fact, I would consider it to be more of a chore! I do most of my shaving in the shower, and I&#x27;m always paranoid that I will clumsily cut myself while trying to get a close shave (it&#x27;s happened many times before). I mostly blame the narrow, pencil width handles that most commercial razors are designed to have. Unlike the traditional woman&#x27;s razor, the Schick Hydro Silk TrimStyle has a thick, substantial handle with a rubber-like grip that is super easy to hold and maneuver, even with wet hands! I didn&#x27;t know how much I would love this design feature, until I&#x27;d successfully and confidently used this razor several times without injury. The smoothness and closeness of the actual shave is also superior to most of the razors I&#x27;ve used in the past. The Hydro Silk TrimStyle has FIVE blades that work seamlessly with the two moisturizer strips (one above the blades and one below). I&#x27;ve found that the five blade styles are most often found on men&#x27;s razors; which I have used in the past. As I mentioned, shaving isn&#x27;t my favorite pastime; so I&#x27;d prefer to get it over with as soon as possible. In the winter months, I hardly ever shave my legs...what&#x27;s the point? The first time I used this part of the razor I removed the trim comb; thinking it was just a cap to cover the blades when you are using the other end. Being a novice at bikini area trimming, I did wonder why the blades (on the trimmer side) were so flat. Does this keep them from getting too dull? I noticed that the trimmer blades cannot be replaced without getting another razor. I don&#x27;t think I will be using this end of the razor very often.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall, I think the Schick Hydro Silk TrimStyle is a great tool! Is there any way to make them last longer? My experience was that the first shave (with a new blade) is a lot closer and smoother than those that follow. Lastly, the product I received did not include a holder piece to mount the razor on a wall. I know that Schick makes these, and the Hydro Silk TrimStyle does have a &#x27;clip&#x27; on one side that looks like it attaches to a holder. I like to keep all of my shower products and tools organized. The wall mounted shower holder would&#x27;ve been nice to have for easier access.Unlike most razors, the blades did not irritate my skin afterwards.
